## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / kinetic ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time-derivative of concentration A, which is the standard setup for kinetic rate-law identification via ordinary differential equations. With only A and t available, the most likely relationships are mass-action consumption/production terms in A and possible time-varying effective rate coefficients k(t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zeroth-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate consumption, e.g., surface-limited or saturated reagent)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive/thermal decomposition, pseudo-first-order)
- Second-order kinetics (single-species): dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (dimerization or bimolecular self-reaction when only A is tracked)
- General n-th order rate law: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical/global reaction order fitting)
- Half-order / fractional-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 with 0 < c1 < 1 (diffusion/chain or complex mechanism lumping)
- Linear relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to steady-state/equilibrium concentration c1)
- Reversible first-order with finite pool: dA_dt = -c0 * A + c1 * (c2 - A) (A interconverts with another state; c2 is total/maximum)
- Autocatalytic (logistic-type) kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating growth with depletion/limit)
- Autocatalysis with background decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (induction/autocatalytic production competing with loss)
- Pseudo-second-order with offset/background: dA_dt = -c0 * A * (A + c1) (effective collision term with baseline concentration scale)
- Time-varying rate coefficient (exponentially drifting conditions): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (e.g., temperature/programmed ramp captured as k(t))
- Aging/deactivation of effective rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (1 + c1 * t) (rate slows over time due to catalyst deactivation or depletion of an unmodeled factor)
- Periodically forced kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A (light/chopping, periodic temperature or mixing effects on k(t))
- Substrate-inhibited / crowding-limited decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (1 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2) (rate reduction at high A due to inhibition/viscosity/complexation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Consumption-only species A typically yields dA_dt < 0 for A > 0, suggesting leading negative sign on dominant terms in A.
- Mass-action mechanisms map to integer powers of A (A, A**2, A**3), while non-integer powers often indicate lumped diffusion/chain or heterogeneous effects.
- If trajectories approach a nonzero plateau, include a restoring term in (A - c) rather than pure power-law decay.
- Autocatalytic/induction behavior is indicated by initially small |dA_dt| at low A, then faster change at intermediate A, often captured by A*(c - A) or (-A + A**2) structures.
- Time-dependent experimental conditions (ramps, catalyst aging) are naturally represented as k(t) multiplying an A-dependent term, i.e., dA_dt = -k(t) * f(A).
- Periodic modulation in observed rates (e.g., illumination cycling) suggests sinusoidal dependence in t multiplying A-dependent kinetics.
- Inhibition/crowding at high A is reflected by rational slow-down factors like 1/(1 + c*A + c*A**2), producing diminishing rate magnitude as A grows.
- Reversible interconversion with a conserved total often appears as a linear combination of A and (c - A), implying two opposing first-order fluxes.

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK18)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_p*sin(c3*A)
Candidate formulas: 55

GT is the fixed function of \(A\) only (no \(t\) dependence):
\[
f(A)= -0.5637231318832533\,A^2 + 0.1313786441969526\sin(0.7616913890711074\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must be able to (i) remove all \(t\)-dependence, (ii) have **no** extra terms like \(A\), constants, logs, exponentials, rational-in-\(A\) artifacts, extra powers, etc., and (iii) realize exactly “quadratic + single sine” (with free coefficients/frequency/phase allowed via parameters).

---

### 1. \(A^2c0 + A + c1\log(Ac2+1)+c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\)
Has an unavoidable \(+A\) term (fixed coefficient 1). GT has no linear term. Cannot match.

### 2. \(A^2c0 + c1\sin(Ac2+c3)\)
This is exactly “quadratic + single sine”. Set:
- \(c0=-0.5637231318832533\)
- \(c1=0.1313786441969526\)
- \(c2=0.7616913890711074\)
- \(c3=0\)
Then candidate equals GT for all \(A\). **Matches.**

### 3. \(\frac{A^2}{Ac0+c1}+\frac{Ac2}{Ac0+c1}+c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\)
Contains rational terms in \(A\) unless denominator is constant. If set \(c0=0\), denominator \(=c1\) constant, then terms become \((1/c1)A^2+(c2/c1)A\). To remove linear term need \(c2=0\), leaving only scaled \(A^2\) plus sine—this could match the quadratic+sine shape. But note the quadratic coefficient would be \(1/c1\), which can be set to \(-0.5637...\) by choosing \(c1=-1/0.5637...\). Then sine term can match via \(c3,c4,c5\). So **also matches** (with \(c0=0,c2=0\)).

### 4. Big expression all over \((Ac0+c1)\)
To avoid rational dependence, need \(c0=0\) so denominator constant \(c1\). Then expression becomes a polynomial in \(A\) plus sine terms divided by constant. But it includes terms like \(A\), \((A+c6)^2\), constants, etc. You could try zeroing many coefficients (set \(c2=c5=c7=c8=c9=0\)) and also kill the linear term by setting the remaining linear numerator coefficient to 0; however there is \(A*c1/(Ac0+c1)\) which with \(c0=0\) becomes \(A\) (since \(A*c1/c1=A\)), unavoidable. GT has no \(A\). Cannot match.

### 5. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{(c3+t)^2}+c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
Has \(t\)-dependent term unless \(c2=0\). Then still has linear term \(Ac1\) removable by \(c1=0\). Then becomes quadratic+sine: can match. **Matches** (set \(c2=0,c1=0\), tune others).

### 6. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\)
Can set \(c1=0,c2=0\) leaving quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 7. \(\frac{Ac0}{Ac1+c2}+A+c3\sin(\cdot)+c6(A+c7)^2+\frac{c8}{Ac1+c2}\)
Contains unavoidable \(+A\). GT has no linear term. Cannot match.

### 8. \(A^2c0 + c1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)\)
Set \(c1=0\) to remove constant; then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 9. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)+c5\)
Choose \(c0=2\) to make \(A^2\), set \(c5=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 10. \(Ac0 + Ac1e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 + c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Has \(t\)-dependence unless \(c1=0\) (or \(c2=0\) still leaves \(Ac1\)). Set \(c1=0\). Then has linear term \(Ac0\) removable by \(c0=0\). Then choose \(c3=2\) and tune \(c4\) for quadratic, plus sine. **Matches.**

### 11. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(\cdot) + \frac{c5}{(c6+t)^2}\)
Remove \(t\)-term by \(c5=0\). Remove linear by \(c1=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 12. \(c0\sin(Ac1+c2)+c3(A+c4)^2\)
Expand square: \(c3(A^2+2c4A+c4^2)\). To avoid linear and constant, set \(c4=0\). Then \(c3A^2 + c0\sin(Ac1+c2)\). Set \(c2=0\) for zero phase. Tune \(c3,c0,c1\). **Matches.**

### 13. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove linear by \(c0=0\). Set \(c1=2\) and tune \(c2\) for quadratic; tune sine. **Matches.**

### 14. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(\cdot)\)
Set \(c1=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 15. \(Ac0 + c1\sin(\cdot)+c4\sin(\cdot)+c7(A+c8)^2\)
Has potentially two sine terms; can set one amplitude to 0 (e.g., \(c4=0\)). Square term expands; to avoid linear/constant set \(c8=0\). Also remove linear \(Ac0\) by \(c0=0\). Then \(c7A^2 + c1\sin(\cdot)\). **Matches.**

### 16. \(Ac0 + c1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5e^{Ac6}\)
Need no exponential: set \(c5=0\). Remove constant \(c1=0\). Remove linear \(Ac0\) by \(c0=0\). Left with sine only—cannot produce the required \(-0.5637A^2\). Could try to get quadratic from exponential via series, but must be exact for all \(A\), impossible. Cannot match.

### 17. \(Ac0 + c1\sin(\cdot)+c4 t^{c5}+c6(A+c7)^2\)
Remove \(t\)-term by \(c4=0\). Remove linear \(Ac0\) by \(c0=0\). Set \(c7=0\) to avoid linear/constant from square. Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 18. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{c2 t+c3}+c4e^{Ac5}+c6\sin(\cdot)+\frac{c9}{c2 t+c3}\)
To remove \(t\)-dependence need \(c1=0,c9=0\) (or \(c2=0\) still leaves constants but then terms become linear in \(A\)). Also must remove exponential: \(c4=0\). Then left with \(Ac0 + c6\sin\). No quadratic. Cannot match.

### 19. \(c0 + c1\sin(\cdot)+ \frac{c4 t}{Ac5+c6}+\frac{c7}{Ac5+c6}+c8(A+c9)^2\)
Remove \(t\)-term by \(c4=0\). Rational term \(\frac{c7}{Ac5+c6}\) must vanish: set \(c7=0\). Remove constant \(c0\) and constant/linear from square by \(c0=0,c9=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 20. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{c2 t+c3}+c4\sin(\cdot)+c7(A+c8)^2+\frac{c9}{c2 t+c3}\)
Remove \(t\)-dependence by \(c1=0,c9=0\). Remove linear \(Ac0\) by \(c0=0\). Set \(c8=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 21. \(c0 + c1\sin(\cdot)+c4\sin(\cdot)+c7(A+c8)^2\)
Set one sine amplitude to 0 (e.g., \(c4=0\)). Remove constant \(c0=0\). Set \(c8=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 22. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2 + c3\sin(\cdot)+c6(A+c7)^2\)
To avoid extra constant set \(c2=0\). But there are two polynomial-type terms: \(A^{c0}c1\) and square term. You can set one to zero (e.g., \(c1=0\)) and use square term for quadratic with \(c7=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 23. \(Ac0 + c1\sin(\cdot)+c4\log(Ac5+1)+c6(A+c7)^2\)
Log term must vanish: \(c4=0\). Remove linear \(Ac0\) by \(c0=0\). Set \(c7=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 24. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3\sin(\cdot)+c6\sin(\cdot)\)
Exponential must vanish: \(c1=0\). Remove linear \(Ac0\) by \(c0=0\). Need only one sine: set \(c6=0\). Then only sine remains, no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 25. \(Ac0 + A c1 + c2e^{Ac3}+c4\sin(\cdot)+c7\)
Exponential must vanish \(c2=0\). Constant \(c7=0\). Then only linear+ sine; can’t get quadratic. Cannot match.

### 26. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{Ac2+c3}+c4+c5\sin(\cdot)+\frac{c8}{Ac2+c3}\)
To avoid rational terms set \(c1=0,c8=0\). Remove constant \(c4=0\). Then \(Ac0 + c5\sin\): no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 27. \(A^3c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + c3\sin(\cdot)\)
Set \(c0=0,c2=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 28. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3\log(Ac4+1)+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Must remove exp/log: \(c1=0,c3=0\). Then \(Ac0 + c5\sin\): no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 29. \(\frac{A^2c0}{Ac1+c2}+\frac{Ac3}{Ac1+c2}+\frac{Ac4}{Ac1+c2}+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
If \(c1=0\), denominator constant \(c2\): gives \((c0/c2)A^2 + ((c3+c4)/c2)A +\) sine. Set \(c3=-c4\) to remove linear. Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 30. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2e^{Ac3}+c4\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove exponential \(c2=0\). Set \(c0=2\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 31. \(Ac0 + \frac{Ac1}{Ac2+c3}+c4\sin(\cdot)+\frac{c7}{Ac2+c3}\)
Remove rational terms \(c1=0,c7=0\). Then \(Ac0 +\) sine; no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 32. \(\frac{A^2c0}{Ac1+c2}+\frac{Ac3}{Ac1+c2}+c4\sin(\cdot)\)
Set \(c1=0\) so denominator constant \(c2\): \((c0/c2)A^2+(c3/c2)A+\) sine. Set \(c3=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 33. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3e^{Ac4}+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove exponential \(c3=0\). Remove linear \(Ac0=0\). Set \(c1=2\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 34. \(Ac0 + Ac1e^{c2 t}+c3e^{Ac4}+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove \(t\)-term \(c1=0\). Remove exponential \(c3=0\). Remove linear \(c0=0\). Left with sine only, no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 35. Same structure as 19 but with leading \(Ac0\) too
\(Ac0 + c1\sin(\cdot)+ \frac{c4 t}{Ac5+c6}+\frac{c7}{Ac5+c6}+c8(A+c9)^2\).
Set \(c4=0,c7=0\) to remove rational/t. Set \(c0=0\). Set \(c9=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 36. \(\frac{A^2c0}{Ac1+c2}+\frac{Ac3}{A+c2}+c4\sin(\cdot)\)
To avoid rational dependence, try \(c1=0\) so first denom constant \(c2\), but second term still \(\frac{Ac3}{A+c2}\) which is not polynomial unless \(c3=0\). Then becomes quadratic+sine. **Matches** (with \(c1=0,c3=0\)).

### 37. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5\log(Ac6+1)\)
Remove log \(c5=0\). Remove linear \(c1=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 38. \(A + c0\sin(\cdot)+c3e^{Ac4}+c5(A+c6)^2\)
Has unavoidable \(+A\). Cannot match.

### 39. \(c0 + c1\sin(\cdot)+c4 t^{c5}+c6(A+c7)^2\)
Remove \(t\)-term \(c4=0\). Remove constant \(c0=0\). Set \(c7=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 40. \(\frac{Ac0}{Ac1+c2}+c3+c4\sin(\cdot)+\frac{c7}{Ac1+c2}+c8(A+c9)^2\)
Remove rational terms by \(c0=0,c7=0\). Remove constant \(c3=0\). Set \(c9=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 41. \(A + c0\sin(\cdot)+c3\sin(\cdot)+c6(A+c7)^2\)
Unavoidable \(+A\). Cannot match.

### 42. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5+c6\log(Ac7+1)\)
Remove constant \(c5=0\). Remove log \(c6=0\). Set \(c0=2\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 43. \(Ac0 + c1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5e^{Ac6}+c7e^{Ac8}\)
Need remove exponentials \(c5=0,c7=0\). Remove constant \(c1=0\). Remove linear \(c0=0\). Left with sine only, no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 44. \(\frac{Ac0}{Ac1+c2}+c3\sin(\cdot)+c6(A+c7)^2+\frac{c8}{Ac1+c2}\)
Remove rational terms \(c0=0,c8=0\). Set \(c7=0\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 45. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3e^{c4 t}+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove \(t\)-term \(c3=0\). Remove exp-in-A \(c1=0\). Remove linear \(c0=0\). Left with sine only, no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 46. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3e^{Ac4}+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove exponentials \(c1=0,c3=0\). Remove linear \(c0=0\). Left with sine only. Cannot match.

### 47. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove exponential \(c1=0\). Then linear+sine; no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 48. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3\log(c4 t+1)+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove exp/log \(c1=0,c3=0\). Then linear+sine; no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 49. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5e^{c6 t}+c7\)
Remove \(t\)-term \(c5=0\). Remove constant \(c7=0\). Set \(c0=2\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 50. \(A + c0\sin(\cdot)+\frac{c3 t}{c4 t+c5}+\frac{c6}{c4 t+c5}+c7(A+c8)^2\)
Unavoidable \(+A\). Cannot match.

### 51. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3 t^{c4}+c5\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove exp and \(t\)-term: \(c1=0,c3=0\). Then linear+sine; no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 52. \(A + c0\sin(\cdot)+c3(A+c4)^2+\frac{c5 t}{Ac6+c7}+\frac{c8}{Ac6+c7}\)
Unavoidable \(+A\). Cannot match.

### 53. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5e^{c6 t}+c7\log(c8 t+1)+c9\)
Remove \(t\)-terms \(c5=0,c7=0\). Remove constant \(c9=0\). Set \(c0=2\). Then quadratic+sine. **Matches.**

### 54. \(Ac0 + Ac1e^{c2 t}+\frac{Ac3}{Ac4+c5}+c6\sin(\cdot)+\frac{c9}{Ac4+c5}\)
Remove \(t\)-term \(c1=0\). Rational terms: to remove \(\frac{c9}{Ac4+c5}\) set \(c9=0\); to remove \(\frac{Ac3}{Ac4+c5}\) either set \(c3=0\) or make denominator constant with \(c4=0\) (then it becomes linear). In any case, remaining terms are linear \(Ac0\) plus sine; no quadratic. Cannot match.

### 55. \(Ac0 + c1e^{Ac2}+c3\sin(c4 t+c5)+c6\sin(\cdot)\)
Remove exp \(c1=0\). Remove \(t\)-sine \(c3=0\). Then linear+sine; no quadratic. Cannot match.
